
-----title
杭州 (出生地)

id='poem_sentence_1_131953'>谁谓忽远役，怀抱无由宣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131953'>况我骨肉亲，与子枝叶连。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131950'>是时吹寒风，晨起驱行车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131950'>仰视天文乖，俯视长江殊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131950'>良友惜远别，执手相踟蹰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131915'>惊波一何骇，返顾令人忧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131892'>却把向来供奉曲，酒边对客续朱弦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131892'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年</a>　回到杭州，有诗寄李鹤田。作品：《寄李鹤田》<br /><a href="javascript: class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131559")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_131558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131558'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131558'>如此湖山正好嬉，游人船上醉如泥。<div 北京

"poem_title_131747")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131747'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131747'>砚笔寂寥空洒泪，管弦呜咽自生哀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131747'>雪寒门户宾朋少，且拨红炉守泰来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131747'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　在大都。尝至卢沟桥，及郊野观猎。本年前后有诗词多首。作品：《斡鲁垛观猎》、《幽州月夜酒边赋西湖月》、《卢沟桥王昭仪见寄回文次韵》、《关山月》、《忆湖上》、《除夕同舍集饮》、《山东飞放》、《幽州除夜醉歌》<div id='poem_132001' id='poem_sentence_1_132001_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_132001'>白旄黄钺左右绕，毡房殿帐东西旋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_132001_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131958'>一朝歌舞成尘土，断础荒宫走狐兔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131958'>月亦伤心不肯明，人亦吞声泪如雨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131958'>西湖月，几度圆，几度缺。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131958'>人生南北岐路多，几度相逢几度别。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131958'>去年月圆时，我在西湖十里荷花香，□<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑衍）</span>□月吞酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131958'>今年月缺时，我在燕山万里来<span class='inlineComment2'>（顾本作未）</span>□□，□酒招月来。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131958'>劝月酒一杯，我酒饮尽□□□□□□饮，胡为乎来哉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131958'>停杯问月月变色，嫌□□□□□窄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131958'>人生如白驹之过隙，若不痛饮真可惜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131958'>□□□物如流水，何如月照金樽里。<div id='poem_sentence_11_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_131958'>首阳二子忍□□，□丘盗蹠成蝼蚁。<div id='poem_sentence_12_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_131958'>我有长鲸吸川口，倒挽银河添我酒。<div id='poem_sentence_13_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_131958'>我酒千年饮不乾，月光与我长相守。<div id='poem_sentence_14_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_131958'>酒酣拔剑斫地歌，钱王宫阙生白波。<div id='poem_sentence_15_131958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_131958'>西湖月，光更多，有酒不饮将如之何。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_131958_comment'></div></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　在大都。度宗愍忌作词。作品：《玉楼春·度宗愍忌长春宫斋醮》<div id='poem_132045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_132045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年12月</a>　在大都。十二月初九日，宋丞相文天祥就义，作诗招魂。作品：《浮丘道人招魂歌》九首。<div id='poem_131972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浮丘道人招魂歌<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注：见《文丞相集》附录。）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131972")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131972'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131972'>有客有客浮丘翁，一生能事今日终。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131972'>齧毡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_131972", 131972, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>雪窖</span>身不容，寸心耿耿摩苍空<span class='inlineComment2'>（顾本作穹）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131972'>睢阳临难气塞充，大呼南八男儿忠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131972'>我公就义何从容，名垂竹帛生英雄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131972'>呜呼一歌兮歌无穷，魂招不来何所从。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131975'>孤儿以忠报罔极，拔舌剖心命何惜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131975'>地结苌弘血成碧，九泉见母无言责。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131975'>呜呼二歌兮歌复忆，魂招不来长叹息。<div inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>不能结。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131971'>天生男儿硬如铁，白刃飞空肢体裂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131971'>此时与汝成永诀，汝于何处收兄骨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131971'>呜呼三歌兮歌声咽，魂招不来泪流血。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131971'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131970'>乱离<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_131970", 131970, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>走窜</span>千里山，荆棘蹲坐肤不完。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131970'>失身被系泪不乾，父闻此语摧心<span class='inlineComment2'>（顾本作肺）</span>肝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131969'>关河丧乱多杀戮，白日驱人夜烧屋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131969'>一双白璧委沟渎，日暮潜行向天哭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131969'>呜呼七歌兮歌不足，魂招不来泪盈掬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131976'>有诗有诗吟啸集，纸上飞蛇喷香汁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131976'>杜陵宝唾手亲拾，沧海月明老珠泣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131976'>天地长留国风什，鬼神护呵六丁立。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年</a>　上年十二月初九日，遣宋宗室徙居上都，元量从行。是年春，出居庸关。作品：《出居庸关》<div id='poem_131920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>出居庸关</a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a id='poem_sentence_2_131920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131920'>群狐正从横，野枭号古树。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131920'>黑云满天飞，白日翳复吐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131920'>移时风扬沙，人马俱失路。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131920'>踌躇默吞声，聊歌远游赋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131920'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_131920_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='1ce50fae023a45548a030addd9f790ea_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>　约在是年春或稍前，元量从宋宗室回大都。尝夜直万安殿，赋诗云“玉堂夜直”，则元量在翰林院或任职。作品：《万安殿夜直》、《幽州除夜》、《送张舍人从军》、《读文山诗稿》、送张总管归广西》、《易水》；《一剪梅·怀旧》、《忆秦娥》七首。<div id='poem_131736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>万安殿夜直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131736")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131736'>凤衔紫诏下云端，千载明良际会难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131736'>金阙早朝天表近，玉堂夜直月光寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131736'>宫衣屡赐恩荣重，御宴时开礼数宽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131736'>却忆玄都人去后，桃花零落倚阑干。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_132056_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　在大都。十月，瀛国公赵㬎奉命往吐蕃学佛法，元量有诗。全太后为尼于正智寺，元量有诗。本年，元量三上书元世祖，得以黄冠南归。别大都，宋旧宫人及燕赵诸公子饯别，元量有诗。作品：《瀛国公入西域为僧号木波讲师》、《全太后为尼》、《幽州会饯》、《余将南归燕赵诸公子携妓把酒饯别醉中作把酒听歌行》二首。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131936'>有酒有歌君亦愁，把酒听歌君亦乐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131936'>我有鹦鹉杯，君有鸬鹚杓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131936'>一杯一杯复一杯，酒尽还沽共君酌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131936'>满堂金玉守者谁，万事何如酒杯好。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131936'>君不见巢父许由空洗耳，伯夷叔齐空饿死。<div id='poem_sentence_9_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131936'>范蠡扁舟挟西子，五湖风浪兼天起。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131936'>又不见相如怀璧空归来，廉颇善饭何壮哉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_131936'>谢安携妓入东山，苍生望望霖雨乾。<div id='poem_sentence_12_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_131936'>把酒劝君饮，请君为我歌。<div id='poem_sentence_13_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_131936'>燕昭筑台金满地，郭隗登台多意气。<div id='poem_sentence_14_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_131936'>刘琨梦里起听鸡，班超万里封侯归。<div id='poem_sentence_15_131936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_131936'>君不见浣花溪头老翁哭，白首为儒守茅屋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_131936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　元量南归，出蓟门，有诗。作品：《出自蓟门行》<div id='poem_131919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>出自蓟门行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131919")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131919'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131919'>出自蓟门行，行行望天北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131919'>何处愁杀人，黑风走沙石。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131919'>华裾者谁子，意气万人敌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131919'>金鞍鞁白马，奋飞虎生翼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131919'>书生尔何为，不草相如檄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131919'>徒有经济心，壮年已斑白。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131919'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_131919_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
正蓝旗

<div class='label1' id='29927e620bca472b92918144ade4b95d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("29927e620bca472b92918144ade4b95d");'><span id='29927e620bca472b92918144ade4b95d_link' 额济纳旗

-----title
张掖
-----detail

-----title
曲阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5089eb63fb9849af92fc3fc8268e209c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5089eb63fb9849af92fc3fc8268e209c");'><span id='5089eb63fb9849af92fc3fc8268e209c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>，46岁</div><div id='5089eb63fb9849af92fc3fc8268e209c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　正月壬午，世祖遣元量为使祀岳渎东海。行前尝召见。元量此行所祀有恒山、华山、嵩山、衡山、泰山、青城山、济渎、孔子庙等，行程凡一万五千里。所到之处，孰先孰后，尚不全明。作品：《北岳降香呈严学士》<div id='poem_131749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北岳降香呈严学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131749")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131749'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131749'>万里溟濛起战埃，翩翩勒马出金台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131749'>同君远使山头去，如朕亲行岳顶来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131749'>野庙横斜挨老树，古碑颠倒枕荒苔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131749'>瞻天只有丹心在，香篆炉熏达九垓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131749'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131749_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
登封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3ad0129d1cd74da89e3edfc273b44016_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3ad0129d1cd74da89e3edfc273b44016");'><span id='3ad0129d1cd74da89e3edfc273b44016_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　祀中岳嵩山，有诗。沿途过孟津、洛阳、北邙、函谷关等地，皆有诗。作品：《嵩山》二首、《》<div id='poem_131996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131996' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131996")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131996'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131996'>客行天地中，嵩峰何突兀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131996'>鸟道阻且修，马烦行复歇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131996'>一入玉女窗，便觉幽兴发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131996'>好鸟鸣嘤嘤，细草乱如发。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131996'>中有神圣居，飞甍半摧折。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》作蹈）</span>仙辙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131996'>徒有感慨怀，脉脉泪不绝。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131996'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_131996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_131996'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_131996_0'>⑴ 《诗渊》册三页二○七○作喷白</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_131996_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_131997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131997?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><br id='poem_sentence_0_131997'>行行太室峰，秋声若鸣镝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131997'>流目瞩崎岖，蓬莱应咫尺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131997'>上有神仙区，下有穆王宅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131997'>徘徊复徘徊，泫然感畴昔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131997'>八骏不重来，秋山空月白。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131997'>安得会璆韶，共作瑶池客。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131997'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_131997_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

华阴

都江堰
-----detail

class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131819")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_131822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131822'>山中老柏滴寒翠，江上危峰撑夕阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
济源
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　祀济渎，有诗。登王屋山绝顶天坛山或在此时。作品：《济渎》、《天坛山》<div id='poem_131834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131834' class='poemTitle href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131834")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131834'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131834'>玉简投潭洞，金樽出石隈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131834'>龙光蟠窟宅，蜃气结楼台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131834'>卷地风雷起，掀天雨雹来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131834'>人间为济渎，水底即蓬莱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131834'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131834_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_131908'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131908'>我登天坛山，洒然清吟目。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131908'>群峰如儿孙，罗列三十六。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131908'>支藤陟曾巅，中有少室屋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131908'>山人化飞仙，庭除生苜蓿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131908'>古碑野火烧，剥落字难读。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131908'>雏鹿卧幽岩，孤鸟响空谷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131908'>解鞍小迟留，偷閒半日足。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131908'>长啸归去来，题诗纪幽独。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131908'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_131908_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='292bd1f9c68e4a63928919fa6aa9f32a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("292bd1f9c68e4a63928919fa6aa9f32a");'><span id='292bd1f9c68e4a63928919fa6aa9f32a_link' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_132011")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_132011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_132011'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_132011'>寻僧入相国寺，领客过太师桥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_132011_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_132011'>行到汴堤西畔，柳阴阴处鱼跳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_132011_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_132011'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_132011_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夷山醉歌<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_131927'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131927'>楚狂醉歌歌正发，更上梁台望明月。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131927'>朔<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛本作西）</span>风猎猎吹我衣，绝代佳人皎如雪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131927'>搥羯鼓，弹箜篌，烹羊宰牛坐糟丘，一笑再笑扬清讴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131927'>遥看汴水波声小，锦棹<span class='inlineComment2'>（《水云集》作缆）</span>忘还事多少。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131927'>昨日金明池上来，艮岳凄凉麋鹿绕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131927'>麦青青，黍离离，万年枝上鸦乱啼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131927'>二龙北狩不复返，六龙南渡无还期。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131927'>金铜泪迸露盘湿，画阑桂柱酸风急。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131927'>鸠居<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_131927", 131927, id='poem_sentence_9_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131927'>吴山日落天沈沈，母子同行向天北。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131927'>关河万里雨露深，小儒何必悲苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_11_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_131927'>归来耳热忘头白，买笑挥金莫相失。<div id='poem_sentence_12_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_131927'>呼奚奴，吹觱篥，美人纵复横，今夕复何夕。<div id='poem_sentence_13_131927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_131927'>楚狂醉歌歌欲辍，老猿为我啼竹裂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_131927_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131926' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131926'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131926'>呜呼再歌兮花满台，好月为我光徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131926'>人生在世不满百，纷华过眼皆成灰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131926'>夷山青青汴水绿，西北高楼咽丝竹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131926'>美人十指纤如玉，为我行觞歌一曲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131926'>含宫嚼徵当窗牖，露脚斜飞湿杨柳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131926'>就中有客话陈桥，如此山河落人手。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131926'>客且住，听我语，楚汉中分两丘土。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131926'>七雄争战总尘埃，三国莺花浩无主。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131926'>咸阳宫殿不复都，华清池沼温泉枯。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131926'>世间兴废奔如电，沧海桑田几回变。<div id='poem_sentence_9_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131926'>人生得意且尽欢，何须苦苦为高官。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131926'>人生有命且行乐，何必区区叹牢落。<div id='poem_sentence_11_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_131926'>遮莫金章与玉珂，何如桐江披钓蓑。<div id='poem_sentence_12_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_131926'>遮莫貂蝉贵此身，何如柴桑漉酒巾。<div id='poem_sentence_13_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_131926'>君不见海上看羊手持节，饥来和雪和毡齧。<div id='poem_sentence_14_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_131926'>又不见饭颗山头人见嗤，愁吟痛饮真吾师。<div id='poem_sentence_15_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_131926'>美人美人劝我酒，有客有客听我歌。<div id='poem_sentence_16_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_131926'>须臾客醉美人睡，我亦不知天与地。<div id='poem_sentence_17_131926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_131926'>呜呼再歌兮无人听，月自落兮酒未醒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_131926_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131902?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_131902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131902'>牛郎织女涉清浅，支机石上今何年。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 涿州

<div class='label1' id='2db7a32a77ca40ddbf6eb1ec5cf35888_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2db7a32a77ca40ddbf6eb1ec5cf35888");'><span id='2db7a32a77ca40ddbf6eb1ec5cf35888_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>，48岁</div><div id='2db7a32a77ca40ddbf6eb1ec5cf35888' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　南归过涿州，有诗。作品：《涿州》<div id='poem_131986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涿州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131986")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131986'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131986'>泸沟桥下水泠泠，落木无边秋正清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131986'>牛马乱铺黄帝野，鹰鹯高摩涿州城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131986'>柳亭日射旌旗影，花馆风传鼓吹声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131986'>归客偶然舒望眼，酒边触景又诗成。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131986'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131986_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
正定
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='95ae44bcdc2042f0b4aafa000d335970_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("95ae44bcdc2042f0b4aafa000d335970");'><span id='95ae44bcdc2042f0b4aafa000d335970_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>，48岁</div><div id='95ae44bcdc2042f0b4aafa000d335970' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　南归过真定，有诗。作品：《真定客舍》<div id='poem_131863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>真定官舍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131863")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131863'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131863'>使君数问夜如何，灯烛高张照绮罗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131863'>白酒千杯浇客醉，红妆一面恼人多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131863'>风烟漠漠庭前树，霜月娟娟沼内荷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131863'>驿吏出门相语及，城南便是滹沱河。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131863'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131863_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

星子

<div class='label1' id='4d49c393d2f64d5999e542b6fd6e57a6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4d49c393d2f64d5999e542b6fd6e57a6");'><span id='4d49c393d2f64d5999e542b6fd6e57a6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>，48岁</div><div id='4d49c393d2f64d5999e542b6fd6e57a6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　南归过星子，有诗。作品：《星子驿别客》<div id='poem_131832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>星子驿别客</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131832")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131832'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131832'>星江彼此系行舟，我向南州君北州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131832'>彭泽初归元亮醉，沙场远使子卿愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131832'>人生离合花间蝶，世事浮沉柳外鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131832'>明日沾襟各分手，相思何处倚高楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131832'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131832_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

衢州

<div class='label1' id='82caa7122d464514bebd3eefe07dbf2c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("82caa7122d464514bebd3eefe07dbf2c");'><span id='82caa7122d464514bebd3eefe07dbf2c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>，49岁</div><div id='82caa7122d464514bebd3eefe07dbf2c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　年初，元量过衢州，与府学王教授唱和。作品：《三衢官舍和王府教》<div id='poem_131737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三衢官舍和王府教</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131737")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131737'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131737'>十年牢落走穷荒，万里归来行路长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131737'>坐上佳宾能鼓瑟，窗前细雨好烧香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131737'>武淹某泽常思汉，甫寓鄜州只念唐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131737'>秉烛相看真梦寐，夜阑无语意茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131737'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131737_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ebc82755a57b4f44b832985a0166e30d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ebc82755a57b4f44b832985a0166e30d");'><span id='ebc82755a57b4f44b832985a0166e30d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>，49岁</div><div id='ebc82755a57b4f44b832985a0166e30d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　春，元量过桐庐钓台，赋诗。作品：《钓台》<div id='poem_131817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钓台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131817")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131817'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131817'>滩沙叠叠是潮痕，古木苍然叫断猿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131817'>此老不干天子贵，故人方讶布衣尊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131817'>雨甜春水鱼龙动，风暖寒林鸟雀喧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131817'>我恰扁舟台下过，桐花香处月黄昏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131817'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131817_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
乐平
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f743453426e64b7e8b3486e7935cada6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f743453426e64b7e8b3486e7935cada6");'><span id='f743453426e64b7e8b3486e7935cada6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>，50岁</div><div id='f743453426e64b7e8b3486e7935cada6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　春，重访马廷鸾于乐平。三月十一日，马廷鸾应请为《湖山类稿》作序。作品：《重访马碧梧》<div id='poem_131843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重访马碧梧</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131843")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131843'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131843'>万里远行役，十年良可哀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131843'>前辈古风在，故人今雨来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131843'>绝口不言事，挽须惟把杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131843'>种得碧梧树，春风花自开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131843'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131843_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
修水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='836a8db12321417bafe345d1655f2500_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("836a8db12321417bafe345d1655f2500");'><span id='836a8db12321417bafe345d1655f2500_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>，50岁</div><div id='836a8db12321417bafe345d1655f2500' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　往分宁，别章鉴。鉴尝为元量诗作序，今不传。作品：《别章杭山》<div id='poem_131938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别章杭山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131938")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131938'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131938'>抱琴曾北向，弹铗复南图。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131938'>李泌游衡岳，知章赐鉴湖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131938'>柱头仙是鹤，濠上子非鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131938'>此夜同联鼎，他年莫寄书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131938'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131938_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
金溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b925e13e7c614b36bdb4e84a77b4823e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b925e13e7c614b36bdb4e84a77b4823e");'><span id='b925e13e7c614b36bdb4e84a77b4823e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>，50岁</div><div id='b925e13e7c614b36bdb4e84a77b4823e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　应曾子良之招，往访其于家乡金溪山中。作品：《曾平山招饮》<div id='poem_131878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾平山招饮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131878")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131878'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131878'>老貌不随俗，固穷而隐居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131878'>一坞百竿竹，八窗千卷书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131878'>酌以旋篘酒，荐之新网鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131878'>兴尽出门去，晚凉山雨馀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131878'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131878_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
岳阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d042ce0dd92544de92a81937b5ceccff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d042ce0dd92544de92a81937b5ceccff");'><span id='d042ce0dd92544de92a81937b5ceccff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>，50岁</div><div id='d042ce0dd92544de92a81937b5ceccff' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　秋，赴湘，重过巴陵，有诗记之。作品：《巴陵》<div id='poem_131910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>巴陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131910")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131910'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131910'>重到巴陵秋正清，岳阳城下系孤舲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131910'>江湖万里水云阔，天地一凉河汉明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131910'>月出洞庭鱼婢舞，气蒸云梦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>雁奴腥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131910'>篙工又鼓潇湘柁，渔笛渔榔上下鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131910'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_131910'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_131910_0'>⑴ 毛本、《诗渊》册三页一九六一作梦泽</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_131910_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
宜昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7190fb74edfd4649bf69a13f4c2bd846_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7190fb74edfd4649bf69a13f4c2bd846");'><span id='7190fb74edfd4649bf69a13f4c2bd846_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>，51岁</div><div id='7190fb74edfd4649bf69a13f4c2bd846' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　是年秋，由湖南经湖北入川，有诗记行。诗中胜迹如贾谊祠、汨罗江、定王台、虞帝庙、杜甫墓等在湖南，黄陵庙、楚王台等在湖北。作品：《竹枝歌》十首。<div id='poem_131556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>竹枝歌<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1291年）</span><span 成都

class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昝相公送锦被</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131962")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131962'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131962'>蜀都府主迎宾客，赠我蜀锦三百尺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131962'>美人蔌蔌弄金梭，鸳鸯机上初成疋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131962'>繁花乱蕊皆同心，艳蘖中含杜鹃血。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131962'>玉妃如霜姑射仙，金刀剪破云霞缬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131962'>为我裁成合欢被，细意密缝无线迹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131962'>道人把玩色相射，银海光摇泪珠滴。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131962'>却忆故家初破时，绣龙画雉如砂石。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131962'>绮窗窈窕花离离，红妆万镜娇无力。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131962'>百幅锦帆风不动，绿湿红鲜荡春碧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131962'>纷华过眼一梦如，蜀锦吴绫复何益。<div id='poem_sentence_9_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131962'>白茅安用红锦包，虎皮难以裹羊质。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131962'>只今卷锦还府主，心地了然无得失。<div id='poem_sentence_11_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_131962'>铜壶漏断银缸灭，昆崙影转初三月。<div id='poem_sentence_12_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_131962'>道人坐久闻妙香，纸帐蒲团自清绝<span class='inlineComment2'>（影印《诗渊》册一页五九）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_131962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_131962'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_131962_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>歌妓许冬冬携酒郊外小集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131891")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131891'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131891'>益州歌妓许冬冬，客里相逢似燕鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131891'>醉拥蜀琴抽白雪，舞回班扇割西风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131891'>山炰野馔荒山里，浪蕊浮花古寺中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131891'>偶尔留连借馀景，出门一笑夕阳红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131891'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131891_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_132000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_132000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/132000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>锦城秋暮海棠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_132000")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_132000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_132000'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_132000'>锦城海棠妙无比，秋光染出胭脂蕊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_132000'>日照殷红如血鲜，箭砂妆粒真珠子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_132000'>玉环著酒睡初觉，脸薄粉香泪如洗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_132000'>绛纱穿露水晶圆，笑杀荷花守红死。<div id='poem_sentence_3_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_132000'>蜀乡海棠根本别，有色有香成二美。<div id='poem_sentence_4_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_132000'>春花开残秋复花，簸弄东君权不已。<div id='poem_sentence_5_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_132000'>锦袍公子汗血驹，宾客諠哗间朱紫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_132000'>有酒如池肉如山，银烛千条照罗绮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_132000'>萧娘十八青丝发，手把金钟歌皓齿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_132000'>神仙艳骨世所无，歌声直入青云里。<div id='poem_sentence_9_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_132000'>江南倦客惨不乐，鸣笛哀筝乱人耳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_132000'>干戈满地行路难，屏里吴山数千里。<div id='poem_sentence_11_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_132000'>遥怜花国化青芜，浪蕊浮花敢欣喜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_132000'>草堂无诗花无德，窃号花仙宁不耻。<div id='poem_sentence_13_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_132000'>春花撩乱亦可怜，秋花烂熳何为尔。<div id='poem_sentence_14_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_132000'>花前妙舞曲未终，红雪纷纷落流水。<div id='poem_sentence_15_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_132000'>薄命佳人只土尘，抛杯拔剑长歌起<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书页二五一七）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_132000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_132000'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_132000_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3c8ecd2dc97049eb8fd6ac262492c382_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3c8ecd2dc97049eb8fd6ac262492c382");'><span id='3c8ecd2dc97049eb8fd6ac262492c382_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>，53岁</div><div id='3c8ecd2dc97049eb8fd6ac262492c382' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年1月5日</a>　游成都元月初五日药市，有诗。作品：《药市》<div id='poem_131586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>药市</a><span class='authorDate'>（1293年1月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131586")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_131586_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_131586'>成都五月，家家列药于市，以为盛事。</div><div id='poem_preface_131586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131586'>蜀乡人是大医王，一道长街尽药香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131586'>天下苍生正狼狈，愿分良剂救膏肓<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书页二二三五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131586'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131586_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
眉山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='479146b86c47463c94ef05900a221733_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("479146b86c47463c94ef05900a221733");'><span id='479146b86c47463c94ef05900a221733_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>，52岁</div><div id='479146b86c47463c94ef05900a221733' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>　游眉州借景亭，有诗。作品：《眉州借景亭》<div id='poem_131965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>眉州借景亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131965")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_131965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131965'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131965'>巍亭借景引壶觞，元祐诗人翰墨香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131965'>苍峡雷霆龙意气，碧崖烟雨豹文章。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131965'>隔邻修竹娟娟静，夹道枯桑冉冉黄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131965'>水泛帘栊檐影倒，风吹城堞角声长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131965'>巴童结束歌仍俊，蜀女腰肢舞亦狂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131965'>千古相望翁季在，眉山草木有辉光<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书册五页三一一四）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131965'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_131965_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
峨眉山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='30f5b42ab67a4126a205fb5f5a216f34_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("30f5b42ab67a4126a205fb5f5a216f34");'><span id='30f5b42ab67a4126a205fb5f5a216f34_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>，52岁</div><div id='30f5b42ab67a4126a205fb5f5a216f34' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>　游峨眉山绝顶光相寺，有诗。作品：《光相寺》<div id='poem_131923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光相寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131923")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131923'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131923'>峨眉县西四十里，峭壁悬崖削寒翠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131923'>崎岖栈道动摇摇，矮石支撑同赑屃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131923'>忽窥万仞黑无底，下有龙渊七十二。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131923'>攀扪步步足难移，大盘小盘八十四。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131923'>行行更入娑罗平，侧立长嗟心胆碎。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131923'>洗脚溪头登土峰，板屋数间光相寺。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131923'>寺中萧然无个僧，普贤小殿生阴气。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131923'>天仙桥上光明岩，银色光中世界异。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131923'>须臾风雨洗天来，兜罗绵云塞天地。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131923'>虚空现出大圆光，五色晕中瞻大士。<div id='poem_sentence_9_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131923'>日暮云收山寂然，乙夜灯分百千计。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131923'>别有草庵三四僧，花木满轩颇清致。<div id='poem_sentence_11_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_131923'>有时云起自雷岩，两道金光出岩际。<div id='poem_sentence_12_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_131923'>有时云散光独明，犹见光中回象辔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_131923'>僧云又有清现光，白日无云光更丽。<div id='poem_sentence_14_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_131923'>奇花异草吹香风，怪兽珍禽左右至。<div id='poem_sentence_15_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_131923'>善财童子何许来，五十三参见真谛。<div id='poem_sentence_16_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_131923'>神通变化无了时，如幻如梦复如戏。<div id='poem_sentence_17_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_131923'>胡为狡狯弄精魂，机事机心极无谓。<div id='poem_sentence_18_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_131923'>儒生持此问山僧，僧曰如是观如是。<div id='poem_sentence_19_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_131923'>若言有相更有光，灵化千千诚小技。<div id='poem_sentence_20_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_131923'>何如无光复无相，湛寂名为第一义。<div id='poem_sentence_21_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_131923'>菩萨空中数点头，收敛圆光无一事。<div id='poem_sentence_22_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_131923'>雪山万点白差差，初日照之光毳毳。<div id='poem_sentence_23_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_131923'>遥瞻天竺立绵延，我欲游观足如系。<div id='poem_sentence_24_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_131923'>平生兹游真冠绝，走笔成诗图快意<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书页三六八二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_25_131923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_131923'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_131923_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广元
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_0_131549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131549'>金刀剪下三千颗，对客从容把酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131549_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131550?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_131550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131550'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131550'>害<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：吴本客）</span>马劳人事已灰，长安无复使臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：吴本人）</span>来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131550'>满园蓊蔚千千树，尽是杨妃死后栽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131550'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131550_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131548?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_131548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131548'>锦树高枝<span class='inlineComment2'>（顾本、毛本作低）</span>种万窠<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：吴本低种万颗）</span>，岁收百斛足生涯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131548'>八钱买得一斤重，鲁直诗中特地誇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131548_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131928?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_131928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131928'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131928'>锦壳中间玉一团，树高数丈实难攀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131928'>泸戎颗颗甜如蜜，夔梓累累味薄酸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131928'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131928_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泸州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3c8b241f695f4ff69be123e5c38af619_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3c8b241f695f4ff69be123e5c38af619");'><span id='3c8b241f695f4ff69be123e5c38af619_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>，53岁</div><div id='3c8b241f695f4ff69be123e5c38af619' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>　是年秋出川，从泸州顺流而下，有诗。作品：《泸州》<div id='poem_131954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泸州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1293年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131954")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_131954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131954'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131954'>复作泸州去，轻舟疾复徐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131954_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131954'>峡深藏虎豹，谷暗隐樵渔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131954_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131954'>西望青羌远，南瞻白帝迂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131954_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131954'>晴<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛本作暗）</span>岚侵簟枕，寒露湿衣裾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131954_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131954'>野沼荷将尽，山园荔已疏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131954_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131954'>长官相见后，置酒斫鲸鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131954_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131954'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_131954_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
江陵
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='755af9693fed4b7194d15f10643efaad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("755af9693fed4b7194d15f10643efaad");'><span id='755af9693fed4b7194d15f10643efaad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>，53岁</div><div id='755af9693fed4b7194d15f10643efaad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>　出川过江陵，有诗。作品：《江陵》<div id='poem_131769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131769?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1293年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36812, "宋末元初", "汪元量", "poem_title_131769")'>汪元量</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131769'>月到荆江上，轻帆莫远扬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131769'>水摇龙影动，风送雁声长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131769'>北斗回秋柄，南辰耿夜光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131769'>徘徊舒一啸，诗兴落潇湘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131769'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131769_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
